Reviewer<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" contain="paint" buffered-rendering="static" viewBox="0 0 16 12" class="c-teal-100 tiny ml-half icon-checkmark-thick nessy-only" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" role="presentation"><path d="M13.333 0L6.667 6.667l-4-4L0 5.333 6.667 12 16 2.667z"></path></svg></div></div><div alt="Validated impact.com/performance Screenshot" class="tag" title="The reviewer uploaded a screenshot or submitted the review in-app verifying them as current user." ue="tooltip"><div class="d-f ai-c">Verified Current User<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" contain="paint" buffered-rendering="static" viewBox="0 0 16 12" class="c-teal-100 tiny ml-half icon-checkmark-thick nessy-only" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" role="presentation"><path d="M13.333 0L6.667 6.667l-4-4L0 5.333 6.667 12 16 2.667z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="tag" data-container="body" title="Organic review. This review was written entirely without invitation or incentive from G2, a seller, or an affiliate." ue="tooltip">Review source: Organic</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-0"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2022-10-02" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2022-10-02">Oct 02, 2022</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/impact-com-performance/reviews/impact-com-performance-review-7158611"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Review by a brand owner - stay away from Impact at all costs"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Customer support is responsive, and we have also received an account manager. However, none of this helped. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">If you think Impact will help you increase your product sales, you are most likely wrong. Yes, there are a few good quality media outlets/influencers listed on Impact, but these will never respond to you or accept your request.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">Other than that, the plaform is filled with "influencers" and portals of extremely low quality with close to zero traffic and cheap websites that you don't even want to be associated with. Also, most of them are from 3rd world countries. Impact has failed to do absolutely any background check on their listed partners.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">That is not all - many of the registered partners are not people interested in promoting products. Instead, they are companies trying to sell you either affiliate program management services or other promotional services for high fees.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">We have also tried to bring influencers from outside of Impact and our impression is that the affiliate market is extremely oversaturated - no decent partner wants to work on affiliate only basis (e.g. getting % from the sale). Instead, they all require a flat fee on top the % from the sale, which makes the whole collaboration unprofitable for you.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">If you still want to try an affiliate program for your brand - at least choose one of the free/low-fee platforms without long-term commitment. We have signed a 12-month contract with Impact with a high monthly fee, and now we're stuck with it. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-7158611 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Impact offers an existing network of affiliates, however most of them are of exteremely low quality. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex Impact is also able to support pretty much any size of advertiser and smaller merchants can scale their programs effectively.  <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The Insights reporting is not always intuitive and their help docs could use more frequent updating to align with changes made to the platform.  <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-2789574 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering impact.com/performance:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Make sure to fully scope out your desired use cases going into the contract discussions, so that you can avoid costly future implementations and identify and learn every feature you'll need to make use of.  <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-2789574 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">We previously had a lot of reporting issues and lacked transparency as to where our revenue was being generated. Impact has helped us solve this.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">In addition to tracking through an affiliate link, we've been able to track our offline channels because of their unique domains tracking.  <span class="spht">Review data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Everything about Impact.com is fantastic. They have many affiliate programs on their platform from big brands, and I love it the best. They have multiple payment methods, and I like that too. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">What I dislike about the platform is that most affiliate programs have set this auto disapproval for specific locations and disapprove my account without checking my website. And they have a fixed $12 fee when using Bank Transfer for withdrawal which I don't like. If they could lower that fee, then it would be great. And sometimes, the application is just ignored, and some of my applications are still pending for months. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5323350 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering impact.com/performance:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">If anyone is thinking of using impact.com then they should go for it. It's one of the best affiliate networks I have come across. You can essentially set up partnerships using rules and conditions that are unique to each partner.  It is extremely flexible. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Robust fraud detection are not included as part of the base subscription fee. Overall, upsell fees for new features (better fraud detection, better analytics, better influencer discovery, etc.) are frustrating considering the premium price for this network. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4967678 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Two reasons we moved to Impact: 1) better in-app tracking capabilities for affiliate partnerships given more complete tracking abilities across web and in-app and 2) flexibility of custom contracts. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a This review was written entirely without invitation or incentive from G2, a seller, or an affiliate." ue="tooltip">Review source: Organic</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-3"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2022-12-08" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2022-12-08">Dec 08, 2022</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/impact-com-performance/reviews/impact-com-performance-review-7478369"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Great when you start, but terrible when leaving"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Their tracking is great, perfect to keep track of your affiliate sales. Lots of stats, lots of options. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">* The system is complicated, especially for affiliate publishers. We received various complaints about how they felt it was difficult to use.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">* Admin of affiliate conversions is great when you use just one currency. When you are active in various countries and track orders in various currencies it gets messy as they use one base currency for the account. When a conversion needs to be updated it is impossible to do. We have had to do conversion updates that even their support couldn't pull off. It was impossible to do.
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">* When you leave Impact to move to a different system their bureaucracy really kicks in. We had a positive balance (overpaid) but it is impossible to get them to pay it out. Even though it is their accounts department that is reminding us, you have a refund waiting as you overpaid. Fine, here are the account details. But then you have to fill out various forms, authorisations and proof that you actually paid the amount that is in your account. Takes months to solve this... Still ongoing. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-7478369 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Affiliate tracking <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized" ue="toggle-class login-modal-toggle"
